<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Privacy Policy for Suntek Energy</h2> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-15003e3 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="15003e3" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">At Suntek Energy, accessible from https://suntekenergy.com.au/, one of our main priorities is the privacy of our visitors. This Privacy Policy document contains types of information that is collected and recorded by Suntek Energy and how we use it.
<br/><br/>
If you have additional questions or require more information about our Privacy Policy, do not hesitate to contact us.<br/><br/>This Privacy Policy applies only to our online activities and is valid for visitors to our website with regards to the information that they shared and/or collect in Suntek Energy.</p> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-5a3cf3a elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="5a3cf3a" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Consent</h2> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-eddff8a elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="eddff8a" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">By using our website, you hereby consent to our Privacy Policy and agree to its terms</p> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-d756ccd elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="d756ccd" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Information we collect</h2> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-c4308bf elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="c4308bf" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">The personal information that you are asked to provide, and the reasons why you are asked to provide it, will be made clear to you at the point we ask you to provide your personal information.<br/><br/>If you contact us directly, we may receive additional information about you such as your name, email address, phone number, the contents of the message and/or attachments you may send us, and any other information you may choose to provide.<br/><br/>When you register for an Account, we may ask for your contact information, including items such as name, company name, address, email address, and telephone number.</p> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-0a4057c elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="0a4057c" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">How we use your information</h2> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-8c9ef02 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="8c9ef02" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">We use the information we collect in various ways, including to:</p> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-def451f elementor-icon-list--layout-traditional elementor-widget elementor-widget-icon-list" data-element_type="widget" data-id="def451f" data-widget_type="icon-list.default">

<span class="elementor-icon-list-icon">
<i aria-hidden="true" class="fas fa-circle"></i> </span>

</li>

<i aria-hidden="true" class="fas fa-circle"></i> </span>
<span class="elementor-icon-list-text">Find and prevent fraud</span>
</li>

</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-da19aee elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="da19aee" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Log Files</h2> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-89a0054 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="89a0054" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Suntek Energy follows a standard procedure of using log files. These files log visitors when they visit websites. All hosting companies do this and a part of hosting services' analytics. The information collected by log files include internet protocol (IP) addresses, browser type, Internet Service Provider (ISP), date and time stamp, referring/exit pages, and possibly the number of clicks. These are not linked to any information that is personally identifiable. The purpose of the information is for analyzing trends, administering the site, tracking users' movement on the website, and gathering demographic information.</p> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-4b2cc2c elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="4b2cc2c" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Cookies and Web Beacons</h2> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-5b8eb32 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="5b8eb32" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Like any other website, Suntek Energy uses 'cookies'. These cookies are used to store information including visitors' preferences, and the pages on the website that the visitor accessed or visited. The information is used to optimize the users' experience by customizing our web page content based on visitors' browser type and/or other information.</p> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-f4f4170 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="f4f4170" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Advertising Partners Privacy Policies</h2> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-37adaa1 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="37adaa1" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">You may consult this list to find the Privacy Policy for each of the advertising partners of Suntek Energy.<br/><br/>Third-party ad servers or ad networks uses technologies like cookies, JavaScript, or Web Beacons that are used in their respective advertisements and links that appear on Suntek Energy, which are sent directly to users' browser. They automatically receive your IP address when this occurs. These technologies are used to measure the effectiveness of their advertising campaigns and/or to personalize the advertising content that you see on websites that you visit.<br/><br/>Note that Suntek Energy has no access to or control over these cookies that are used by third-party advertisers.</p> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-67df7d2 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="67df7d2" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Third Party Privacy Policies</h2> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-bcdee55 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="bcdee55" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Suntek Energy's Privacy Policy does not apply to other advertisers or websites. Thus, we are advising you to consult the respective Privacy Policies of these third-party ad servers for more detailed information. It may include their practices and instructions about how to opt-out of certain options.<br/><br/>You can choose to disable cookies through your individual browser options. To know more detailed information about cookie management with specific web browsers, it can be found at the browsers' respective websites.</p> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-fe47c44 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="fe47c44" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">CCPA Privacy Rights (Do Not Sell My Personal Information)</h2> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-737d96c elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="737d96c" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Under the CCPA, among other rights, California consumers have the right to:</p> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-ddc47a8 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="ddc47a8" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Request that a business that collects a consumer's personal data disclose the categories and specific pieces of personal data that a business has collected about consumers.</p> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-9250a2f elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="9250a2f" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Request that a business delete any personal data about the consumer that a business has collected.</p> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-cbaaff0 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="cbaaff0" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Request that a business that sells a consumer's personal data, not sell the consumer's personal data.</p> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-68ec72b elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="68ec72b" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">If you make a request, we have one month to respond to you. If you would like to exercise any of these rights, please contact us.</p> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-05d7e3d elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="05d7e3d" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">GDPR Data Protection Rights</h2> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-68afb4b elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="68afb4b" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">We would like to make sure you are fully aware of all of your data protection rights. Every user is entitled to the following:</p> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-fe5326c elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="fe5326c" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">The right to access – You have the right to request copies of your personal data. We may charge you a small fee for this service.</p> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-91dfe00 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="91dfe00" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">The right to rectification – You have the right to request that we correct any information you believe is inaccurate. You also have the right to request that we complete the information you believe is incomplete.</p> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-1a0065f elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="1a0065f" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">The right to erasure – You have the right to request that we erase your personal data, under certain conditions.</p> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-eab5d62 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="eab5d62" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">The right to restrict processing – You have the right to request that we restrict the processing of your personal data, under certain conditions.</p> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-56fd84e elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="56fd84e" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">The right to object to processing – You have the right to object to our processing of your personal data, under certain conditions.</p> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-99057bb elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="99057bb" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">The right to data portability – You have the right to request that we transfer the data that we have collected to another organization, or directly to you, under certain conditions.</p> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-e487c89 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="e487c89" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">If you make a request, we have one month to respond to you. If you would like to exercise any of these rights, please contact us.</p> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-e025e0f elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="e025e0f" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Children's Information</h2> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-0851e52 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="0851e52" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Another part of our priority is adding protection for children while using the internet. We encourage parents and guardians to observe, participate in, and/or monitor and guide their online activity.</p> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-fd1000d elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="fd1000d" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Suntek Energy does not knowingly collect any Personal Identifiable Information from children under the age of 13. If you think that your child provided this kind of information on our website, we strongly encourage you to contact us immediately and we will do our best efforts to promptly remove such information from our records.</p> </div>
</div>
